SELECT s."Id", s."CategoryId", s."CreatedAt", s."Description", s."Name", s."Status", s."VendorId", s."Id0", s."ApprovedAt", s."Description0", s."GSTNumber", s."IsActive", s."LogoUrl", s."PANNumber", s."Status0", s."StoreEmail", s."StoreName", s."UserId", s."Id1", s."Name0", s."ParentId", s."isActive0", s.slug, s0."Id", s0."AvailableValues", s0."IsActive", s0."IsDefault", s0."Price", s0."ProductId", s0."StockQty", s0."Id0", s0."ImageOrder", s0."ImageUrl", s0."VariantId"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."CategoryId", p."CreatedAt", p."Description", p."Name", p."Status", p."VendorId", v."Id" AS "Id0", v."ApprovedAt", v."Description" AS "Description0", v."GSTNumber", v."IsActive", v."LogoUrl", v."PANNumber", v."Status" AS "Status0", v."StoreEmail", v."StoreName", v."UserId", c."Id" AS "Id1", c."Name" AS "Name0", c."ParentId", c."isActive" AS "isActive0", c.slug
    FROM products AS p
    INNER JOIN vendors AS v ON p."VendorId" = v."Id"
    INNER JOIN categories AS c ON p."CategoryId" = c."Id"
    WHERE p."Id" = @id
    LIMIT 1
) AS s
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p0."Id", p0."AvailableValues", p0."IsActive", p0."IsDefault", p0."Price", p0."ProductId", p0."StockQty", p1."Id" AS "Id0", p1."ImageOrder", p1."ImageUrl", p1."VariantId"
    FROM product_variants AS p0
    LEFT JOIN product_images AS p1 ON p0."Id" = p1."VariantId"
    WHERE p0."IsActive"
) AS s0 ON s."Id" = s0."ProductId"
ORDER BY s."Id", s."Id0", s."Id1", s0."Id", s0."ImageOrder"

SELECT p1."Id", p1."CategoryId", p1."CreatedAt", p1."Description", p1."Name", p1."Status", p1."VendorId", v."Id", v."ApprovedAt", v."Description", v."GSTNumber", v."IsActive", v."LogoUrl", v."PANNumber", v."Status", v."StoreEmail", v."StoreName", v."UserId", c."Id", c."Name", c."ParentId", c."isActive", c.slug, s."Id", s."AvailableValues", s."IsActive", s."IsDefault", s."Price", s."ProductId", s."StockQty", s."Id0", s."ImageOrder", s."ImageUrl", s."VariantId"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."CategoryId", p."CreatedAt", p."Description", p."Name", p."Status", p."VendorId", (
        SELECT min(p0."Price")
        FROM product_variants AS p0
        WHERE p."Id" = p0."ProductId" AND p0."IsActive") AS c
    FROM products AS p
    WHERE p."Status" = 'Active'
    ORDER BY (
        SELECT min(p0."Price")
        FROM product_variants AS p0
        WHERE p."Id" = p0."ProductId" AND p0."IsActive") DESC
    LIMIT @p OFFSET @p
) AS p1
INNER JOIN vendors AS v ON p1."VendorId" = v."Id"
INNER JOIN categories AS c ON p1."CategoryId" = c."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p2."Id", p2."AvailableValues", p2."IsActive", p2."IsDefault", p2."Price", p2."ProductId", p2."StockQty", p3."Id" AS "Id0", p3."ImageOrder", p3."ImageUrl", p3."VariantId"
    FROM product_variants AS p2
    LEFT JOIN product_images AS p3 ON p2."Id" = p3."VariantId"
) AS s ON p1."Id" = s."ProductId"
ORDER BY p1.c DESC, p1."Id", v."Id", c."Id", s."Id"

SELECT p0."Id", p0."CategoryId", p0."CreatedAt", p0."Description", p0."Name", p0."Status", p0."VendorId", v."Id", v."ApprovedAt", v."Description", v."GSTNumber", v."IsActive", v."LogoUrl", v."PANNumber", v."Status", v."StoreEmail", v."StoreName", v."UserId", c."Id", c."Name", c."ParentId", c."isActive", c.slug, s."Id", s."AvailableValues", s."IsActive", s."IsDefault", s."Price", s."ProductId", s."StockQty", s."Id0", s."ImageOrder", s."ImageUrl", s."VariantId"

    SELECT p."Id", p."CategoryId", p."CreatedAt", p."Description", p."Name", p."Status", p."VendorId"
    FROM products AS p
    WHERE p."Status" = 'Active'
    ORDER BY p."CreatedAt"
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS p0
INNER JOIN vendors AS v ON p0."VendorId" = v."Id"

    SELECT p1."Id", p1."AvailableValues", p1."IsActive", p1."IsDefault", p1."Price", p1."ProductId", p1."StockQty", p2."Id" AS "Id0", p2."ImageOrder", p2."ImageUrl", p2."VariantId"

) AS s ON p0."Id" = s."ProductId"

SELECT p1."Id", p1."CategoryId", p1."CreatedAt", p1."Description", p1."Name", p1."Status", p1."VendorId", v."Id", v."ApprovedAt", v."Description", v."GSTNumber", v."IsActive", v."LogoUrl", v."PANNumber", v."Status", v."StoreEmail", v."StoreName", v."UserId", c."Id", c."Name", c."ParentId", c."isActive", c.slug, s."Id", s."AvailableValues", s."IsActive", s."IsDefault", s."Price", s."ProductId", s."StockQty", s."Id0", s."ImageOrder", s."ImageUrl", s."VariantId"

SELECT p1."Id", p1."CategoryId", p1."CreatedAt", p1."Description", p1."Name", p1."Status", p1."VendorId", v."Id", v."ApprovedAt", v."Description", v."GSTNumber", v."IsActive", v."LogoUrl", v."PANNumber", v."Status", v."StoreEmail", v."StoreName", v."UserId", c."Id", c."Name", c."ParentId", c."isActive", c.slug, s."Id", s."AvailableValues", s."IsActive", s."IsDefault", s."Price", s."ProductId", s."StockQty", s."Id0", s."ImageOrder", s."ImageUrl", s."VariantId"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."CategoryId", p."CreatedAt", p."Description", p."Name", p."Status", p."VendorId", (
        SELECT min(p0."Price")
        FROM product_variants AS p0
        WHERE p."Id" = p0."ProductId" AND p0."IsActive") AS c
    FROM products AS p
    WHERE p."Status" = 'Active'
    ORDER BY (
        SELECT min(p0."Price")
        FROM product_variants AS p0
        WHERE p."Id" = p0."ProductId" AND p0."IsActive")
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS p1
INNER JOIN vendors AS v ON p1."VendorId" = v."Id"
INNER JOIN categories AS c ON p1."CategoryId" = c."Id"

    SELECT p2."Id", p2."AvailableValues", p2."IsActive", p2."IsDefault", p2."Price", p2."ProductId", p2."StockQty", p3."Id" AS "Id0", p3."ImageOrder", p3."ImageUrl", p3."VariantId"

) AS s ON p1."Id" = s."ProductId"
